      !(function() {
        // when updating this list, also update /src/Common/Locale/Locale.js
        var locales = [
          'en-US',
          'en-GB',
          'en-AU',
          'cs-CZ',
          'de-DE',
          'el-GR',
          'es-ES',
          'es-AR', // NOTE: need to translate to es-MX as done in getLocaleFromNavigator
          'es-MX',
          'fr-FR',
          'hu-HU',
          'it-IT',
          'pl-PL',
          'pt-BR',
          'ro-RO',
          'ru-RU',
          'tr-TR',
          'ja-JP',
          'ko-KR',
          'zh-TW',
          'th-TH',
          'en-PH',
          'en-SG',
          'id-ID',
          'vi-VN'
        ]

        var getLocaleFromNavigator = function() {
          if (navigator.language) {
            if (locales.indexOf(navigator.language) !== -1) {
              if (navigator.language === 'es-AR') return 'es-MX'
              return navigator.language
            }

            for (var j = 0; j < locales.length; j++) {
              var languageSubstring = navigator.language.substr(0, 2)
              if (
                languageSubstring !== 'en' &&
                languageSubstring !== 'es' &&
                locales[j].substr(0, 2) === languageSubstring
              ) {
                return locales[j]
              }
            }
          }

          if (navigator.languages) {
            // match full locale "en-US"
            for (var i = 0; i < navigator.languages.length; i++) {
              if (locales.indexOf(navigator.languages[i]) !== -1) {
                if (navigator.languages[i] === 'es-AR') return 'es-MX'
                return navigator.languages[i]
              }
            }
          }

          if (navigator.languages) {
            // match partial locale (just language) "en"
            for (var i = 0; i < navigator.languages.length; i++) {
              for (var j = 0; j < locales.length; j++) {
                if (
                  locales[j].substr(0, 2) ===
                  navigator.languages[i].substr(0, 2)
                ) {
                  return locales[j]
                }
              }
            }
          }
        }

        /*
         * Sets the webpage's locale based on the following, in priority order:
         * 1. Locale from localStorage (set using riotbar locale switcher)
         * 2. Locale from the Geolambda
         * 3. Locale from navigator.language(s)
         * 4. Default locale (currently 'en-US')
         */
        var selectedLocale = localStorage.getItem('selected-locale')

        // window._geoinfo is initialized on main index.html file in
        // location.js file distributed by the Geolambda
        var geoLocale =
          window._geoinfo &&
          locales.indexOf(window._geoinfo.locale) > -1 &&
          window._geoinfo.locale

        var localeFromNavigator = getLocaleFromNavigator()

        var defaultLocale = 'en-US'

        var suggestedLocale = geoLocale || localeFromNavigator || defaultLocale
        var locale = selectedLocale || suggestedLocale

        var htmlTag = document.getElementsByTagName('html')

        // make sure the locales are using - instead of _
        locale = locale.replace('_', '-')
        suggestedLocale = suggestedLocale.replace('_', '-')

        localStorage.setItem('suggested-locale', suggestedLocale)

        if (htmlTag && htmlTag[0]) {
          /*
           * Adding the lang attribute makes css text-transform: uppercase|captalize
           * work properly with Turkish and possibly other languages
           */
          htmlTag[0].setAttribute('lang', locale)
        }

        /*
         * Load serviceWorker
         */
        if ('serviceWorker' in navigator) {
          // Uninstall service worker
          // TODO: remove this code after a while
          navigator.serviceWorker
            .getRegistrations()
            .then(function(registrations) {
              for (var i = 0; i < registrations.length; i++) {
                registrations[i].unregister()
              }
            })
        }

        // load selected locale synchronously as we need it before anything else
        var request = new XMLHttpRequest()
        request.open(
          'GET',
          '/locale/' + locale + '.json?v=0.1.2166',
          false
        )
        request.send('')
        window._localeStrings = JSON.parse(request.responseText)

        window._appVersion = '0.1.2166'
